Low-confidence detections\n    (confidence < 0.7) are flagged for human review.\n\n    Multiple variables from a single deliverable are all returned.\n    Documentation-only deliverables are excluded.\n    \"\"\"\n    results: list[DetectionResult] = []\n\n    for d in deliverables:\n        desc = d.description\n        if not desc or not desc.strip():\n            continue\n\n        # Documentation suppression\n        if _DOC_SUPPRESSION_RE.search(desc) and not _has_strong_state_signal(desc):\n            continue\n\n        found = _detect_from_description(desc, d.id)\n        results.extend(found)\n\n    return results\n\n\ndef _has_strong_state_signal(desc: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if description has strong state variable signals despite doc verbs.\"\"\"\n    lower = desc.lower()\n    if _SELF_FIELD_RE.search(lower):\n        return True\n    for keyword in (\"counter\", \"offset\", \"cursor\", \"flag\", \"replace\"):\n        if keyword in lower:\n            return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _detect_from_description(desc: str, deliverable_id: str) -> list[DetectionResult]:\n    \"\"\"Extract state variable detections from a single description.\"\"\"\n    results: list[DetectionResult] = []\n    seen_vars: set[str] = set()\n\n    # 1. self._field patterns (highest confidence)\n    for match in _SELF_FIELD_RE.finditer(desc):\n        var_name = match.group(1)\n        if var_name not in seen_vars:\n            seen_vars.add(var_name)\n            results.append(DetectionResult(\n                variable_name=var_name,\n                deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n                introduction_type=IntroductionType.SELF_ASSIGNMENT,\n                confidence=0.95,\n            ))\n\n    # 2. Explicit introduction patterns\n    for pattern, intro_type, confidence in _INTRO_PATTERNS:\n        for match in pattern.finditer(desc):\n            var_name = match.group(1).strip() if match.group(1) else intro_type.value\n            if not var_name:\n                var_name = intro_type.value\n            if var_name not in seen_vars:\n                seen_vars.add(var_name)\n                results.append(DetectionResult(\n                    variable_name=var_name,\n                    deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n                    introduction_type=intro_type,\n                    confidence=confidence,\n                ))\n\n    # 3. _signal_1_invariant_cross_reference(\n    description: str,\n    deliverable_id: str,\n    domain: InputDomain,\n    invariant_lookup: dict[str, InvariantEntry],\n) -> FMEAFailureMode | None:\n    \"\"\"Signal 1: Cross-reference against invariant predicates.\n\n    Violation without error path = silent corruption.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not invariant_lookup:\n        return None\n\n    desc_lower without invariant predicates registered.\n    \"\"\"\n    has_error_path = bool(_ERROR_PATH_RE.search(description))\n    has_return = bool(_SILENT_RETURN_RE.search(description))\n    has_wrong = DomainCategory.ZERO,\n        DomainCategory.NEGATIVE, DomainCategory.FILTER_ALL,\n    }\n    is_degenerate = domain.category in degenerate_categories\n\n    if has_error_path:\n        # Explicit description=(\n                f\"Error path exists for {domain.description} input. \"\n                f\"Detection: immediate.\"\n            ),\n        )\n\n    if has_wrong or (has_mutation and         ),\n        )\n\n    if has_return and is_degenerate and not has_error_path:\n        # Returns value on degenerate input without error\n        detection = DetectionDifficulty.DELAYED if detection_difficulty=result.detection_difficulty,\n                severity=Severity.WRONG_STATE,\n                signal_source=result.signal_source,\n                description=result.description,\n                invariant_predicate=result.invariant_predicate,\n            )\n\n    return result\n\n\ndef _infer_severity_from_description(description: str) -> \"delete\")):\n        return Severity.DATA_LOSS\n    if any(kw in desc_lower for kw in (\"wrong\", \"incorrect\", \"invalid state\", \"mismatch\")):\n        return Severity.WRONG_STATE\n    if \"\"\"Signal 1: Cross-reference against invariant predicates.\n\n    Violation without error path = silent corruption.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not invariant_lookup:\n        return None\n\n    desc_lower = description.lower()\n\n    for var_name, entry in invariant_lookup.items():\n        var_lower = var_name.lower().lstrip(\"_\")\n        if var_lower not in desc_lower and var_name.lower() not in desc_lower:\n            continue\n\n        # Variable referenced in this deliverable\n        has_mutation = bool(_STATE_MUTATION_RE.search(description))\n        has_error_path = bool(_ERROR_PATH_RE.search(description))\n\n        if has_mutation and not has_error_path:\n            # Mutation without error handling = potential invariant violation\n            return FMEAFailureMode(\n                deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n                domain_description=domain.description,\n                detection_difficulty=DetectionDifficulty.SILENT,\n                severity=Severity.WRONG_STATE,\n                signal_source=\"signal_1\",\n                description=(\n                    f\"State variable '{var_name}' mutated without error path. \"\n                    f\"Invariant '{entry.invariant_predicate}' may be violated \"\n                    f\"on {domain.description} input.\"\n                ),\n                invariant_predicate=entry.invariant_predicate,\n            )\n\n    return None\n\n\ndef _signal_2_no_error_path(\n    description: str,\n    deliverable_id: str,\n    domain: InputDomain,\n) -> FMEAFailureMode | None:\n    \"\"\"Signal 2: Independent no-error-path detection.\n\n    Computation returns value on degenerate input without exception = potential silent corruption.\n    Works even without invariant predicates registered.\n    \"\"\"\n    has_error_path = bool(_ERROR_PATH_RE.search(description))\n    has_return = bool(_SILENT_RETURN_RE.search(description))\n    has_wrong = bool(_WRONG_OUTCOME_RE.search(description))\n    has_mutation = bool(_STATE_MUTATION_RE.search(description))\n    has_delayed = bool(_DELAYED_DETECTION_RE.search(description))\n\n    # Degenerate domain categories that are high-risk for silent failures\n    from .fmea_domains import DomainCategory\n\n    degenerate_categories = {\n        DomainCategory.EMPTY, DomainCategory.NULL, DomainCategory.ZERO,\n        DomainCategory.NEGATIVE, DomainCategory.FILTER_ALL,\n    }\n    is_degenerate = domain.category in degenerate_categories\n\n    if has_error_path:\n        # Explicit error handling -> immediate detection\n        severity = _infer_severity_from_description(description)\n        return FMEAFailureMode(\n            deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n            domain_description=domain.description,\n            detection_difficulty=DetectionDifficulty.IMMEDIATE,\n            severity=severity,\n            signal_source=\"signal_2\",\n            description=(\n                f\"Error path exists for {domain.description} input. \"\n                f\"Detection: immediate.\"\n            ),\n        )\n\n    if has_wrong or (has_mutation and not has_error_path and is_degenerate):\n        # Wrong outcome pattern or mutation without error on degenerate input\n        return FMEAFailureMode(\n            deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n            domain_description=domain.description,\n            detection_difficulty=DetectionDifficulty.SILENT,\n            severity=Severity.WRONG_STATE if has_mutation else Severity.DEGRADED,\n            signal_source=\"signal_2\",\n            description=(\n                f\"No error path for {domain.description} input. \"\n                f\"Computation may produce wrong result silently.\"\n            ),\n        )\n\n    if has_return and is_degenerate and not has_error_path:\n        # Returns value on degenerate input without error\n        detection = DetectionDifficulty.DELAYED if has_delayed else DetectionDifficulty.SILENT\n        return FMEAFailureMode(\n            deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n            domain_description=domain.description,\n            detection_difficulty=detection,\n            severity=Severity.DEGRADED,\n            signal_source=\"signal_2\",\n            description=(\n                f\"Returns value on {domain.description} input without error handling. \"\n                f\"Potential silent failure.\"\n            ),\n        )\n\n    return None\n\n\ndef _combine_signals(\n    s1: FMEAFailureMode | None,\n    s2: FMEAFailureMode | None,\n    deliverable_id: str,\n    domain: InputDomain,\n) -> FMEAFailureMode | None:\n    \"\"\"Combine Signal 1 and Signal 2 into unified classification.\n\n    Silent corruption from either signal = highest severity.\n    \"\"\"\n    if s1 is None and s2 is None:\n        return None\n\n    if s1 is not None and s2 is not None:\n        # Both signals fired -- take the more severe classification\n        combined_difficulty = (\n            DetectionDifficulty.SILENT\n            if s1.detection_difficulty == DetectionDifficulty.SILENT\n            or s2.detection_difficulty == DetectionDifficulty.SILENT\n            else max(\n                s1.detection_difficulty,\n                s2.detection_difficulty,\n                key=lambda d: {\"immediate\": 0, \"delayed\": 1, \"silent\": 2}[d.value],\n            )\n        )\n        combined_severity = max(s1.severity, s2.severity)\n\n        # Silent corruption = always highest severity (wrong_state minimum)\n        if combined_difficulty == DetectionDifficulty.SILENT:\n            if combined_severity < Severity.WRONG_STATE:\n                combined_severity = Severity.WRONG_STATE\n\n        return FMEAFailureMode(\n            deliverable_id=deliverable_id,\n            domain_description=domain.description,\n            detection_difficulty=combined_difficulty,\n            severity=combined_severity,\n            signal_source=\"both\",\n            description=(\n                f\"Dual signal detection: {s1.description} | {s2.description}\"\n            ),\n            invariant_predicate=s1.invariant_predicate,\n        )\n\n    # Single signal\n    result = s1 if s1 is not None else s2\n    assert result is not None\n\n    # Silent corruption from any single signal = elevated to wrong_state minimum\n    if result.detection_difficulty == DetectionDifficulty.SILENT:\n        if result.severity < Severity.WRONG_STATE:\n            result = FMEAFailureMode(\n                deliverable_id=result.deliverable_id,\n                domain_description=result.domain_description,\n                detection_difficulty=result.detection_difficulty,\n                severity=Severity.WRONG_STATE,\n                signal_source=result.signal_source,\n                description=result.description,\n                invariant_predicate=result.invariant_predicate,\n            )\n\n    return result\n\n\ndef _infer_severity_from_description(description: str) -> Severity:\n    \"\"\"Infer severity from description keywords.\"\"\"\n    desc_lower = description.lower()\n\n    if any(kw in desc_lower for kw in (\"data loss\", \"corrupt\", \"destroy\", \"delete\")):\n        return Severity.DATA_LOSS\n    if any(kw in desc_lower for kw in (\"wrong\", \"incorrect\", \"invalid state\", \"mismatch\")):\n        return Severity.WRONG_STATE\n    if any(kw in desc_lower for kw in (\"slow\", \"degraded\", \"suboptimal\", \"partial\")):\n        return Severity.DEGRADED\n    return Severity.COSMETIC\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

D-0025: FMEA Deliverable Promotion Specification\n\n## Module\n`src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_promotion.py`\n\n## Promotion Logic\n- Failure modes at/above `wrong_state` severity → promoted to `fmea_test` deliverable\n- Below threshold → recorded as accepted risk in metadata with rationale\n- Silent corruption findings → trigger Release Gate Rule 1\n\n## Promotion Threshold\n- Default: --- Invariant Registry Sub-Pass ---\n    invariant_output = run_invariant_registry_pass(\n        source_deliverables,\n        max_checks_per_variable=max_checks_per_variable,\n    )\n\n    # --- FMEA Sub-Pass ---\n    # Step 1: Enumerate input domains for computational deliverables\n    domain_map = enumerate_all_domains(source_deliverables, max_domains=max_fmea_domains)\n\n    # Step 2: Classify failure modes using dual-signal detection\n    failure_modes = classify_failure_modes(\n        source_deliverables,\n        domain_map,\n        invariant_entries=invariant_output.entries,\n    )\n\n    # Step 3: Promote above-threshold failure modes\n    promotion_output = promote_failure_modes(\n        failure_modes,\n        promotion_threshold=promotion_threshold,\n    )\n\n    # --- Cross-Linking ---\n    _cross_link_invariant_to_fmea(\n        invariant_output.entries,\n        promotion_output.promoted_deliverables,\n    )\n\n    # --- Combine Generated Deliverables ---\n    all_generated = (\n        list(invariant_output.generated_deliverables)\n        + list(promotion_output.promoted_deliverables)\n    )\n\n    # --- Render Combined Section ---\n    section = _render_combined_section(\n        invariant_output, failure_modes, promotion_output,\n    )\n\n    return CombinedM2Output(\n        invariant_output=invariant_output,\n        failure_modes=failure_modes,\n        promotion_output=promotion_output,\n        all_generated_deliverables=all_generated,\n        section_markdown=section,\n    )\n\n\ndef _cross_link_invariant_to_fmea(\n    entries: list[InvariantEntry],\n    fmea_deliverables: list[Deliverable],\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Cross-link invariant entries to corresponding fmea_test deliverables.\n\n    Adds fmea_test deliverable IDs to InvariantEntry metadata (in-place).\n    \"\"\"\n    for entry in entries:\n        linked_fmea_ids = []\n        for d in fmea_deliverables:\n            source_id = d.metadata.get(\"source_deliverable_id\", \"\")\n            invariant_pred = d.metadata.get(\"invariant_predicate\", \"\")\n\n            # Link if the fmea_test references a deliverable in this entry's mutation sites\n            mutation_ids = {ms.deliverable_id for ms in entry.mutation_sites}\n            if source_id in mutation_ids or invariant_pred == entry.invariant_predicate:\n                linked_fmea_ids.append(d.id)\n\n        if linked_fmea_ids:\n            # Store cross-link in the entry's verification_deliverable_ids\n            for fid in linked_fmea_ids:\n                if fid not in entry.verification_deliverable_ids:\n                    entry.verification_deliverable_ids.append(fid)\n\n\ndef _render_combined_section(\n    invariant_output: InvariantRegistryOutput,\n    failure_modes: list[FMEAFailureMode],\n    promotion_output: FMEAPromotionOutput,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Render combined M2 section as markdown.\"\"\"\n    lines = [\"## M2: State Variable Invariant Registry and FMEA Analysis\", \"\"]\n\n    # Invariant registry subsection\n    lines.append(invariant_output.section_markdown)\n    lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # FMEA failure modes table\n    if failure_modes:\n        lines.append(\"### FMEA Failure Mode Table\")\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        lines.append(\"| Deliverable | Domain | Detection | Severity | Signal |\")\n        lines.append(\"|-------------|--------|-----------|----------|--------|\")\n        for fm in failure_modes:\n            lines.append(\n                f\"| {fm.deliverable_id} | {fm.domain_description} | \"\n                f\"{fm.detection_difficulty.value} | {fm.severity.value} | \"\n                f\"{fm.signal_source} |\"\n            )\n        lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # Promotion section\n    lines.append(promotion_output.section_markdown)\n\n    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
